#  The Azerbaijani Declaration of Independence
#########################################################################
event = { 
	id = 2007005
	random = no
	country = AZB

	trigger = {
		event = 2007165 #The August Coup Fails
		event = 2007097 #The Azerbaijani Declaration of Sovereignty
	}
	
	date = { day = 17 month = october year = 1991 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 21 month = december year = 2012 }
	
	name = "azeri_independence"
	desc = "azeri_independence_desc"
	style = 1
	picture = "azerbaijan"
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		command = { type = dissent value = -10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007006 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { OR = { event = 2007166 event = 2007167 } } } type = access which = SOV }
	}
}
#Soviet receives the news

	style = 1
	picture = "azerbaijan_ssr"
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = name where = -1 which = TAG_AZB }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007008 }
	}
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_NO_NEED"
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = dissent value = 3 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2007015
	random = no
	country = SOV
	style = 2
	
	trigger = {
		headofstate = 99900 
	}

	date = { day = 9 month = march year = 1985 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 21 month = december year = 2012 }

	name = "CHERNENKO_DEATH"
	desc = "CHERNENKO_DEATH_DESC"
	picture = "konstantin_chernenko_death"

	action = { trigger = { OR =  { AND = { ai = yes flag = tpstandard } ai = no } }
		name = "APPOINT_GORBACHEV"
		ai_chance = 90
		command = { type = headofstate which = 99910 }
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 99911 }
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 99900 }
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 99901 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = -3 }
	}
	action = { trigger = { OR =  { AND = { ai = yes flag = tpstandard } ai = no } }
		name = "APPOINT_ROMANOV"
		ai_chance = 9
		command = { type = headofstate which = 99910 }
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 99917 }
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 99900 }
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 99901 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	}

	}

		#ai_chance = 90
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }

	}

		command = { type = dissent value = 20 }

#########################################################################
#  Law on Joint Ventures
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 2007018
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = { 
		headofgovernment = 99911 #Gorbachev
		event = 2007021 #Glasnost
	}
	
	date = { day = 0 month = june year = 1987 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = january year = 1990 }
	
	name = "sov_law_joint_ventures"
	desc = "sov_law_joint_ventures_desc"
	style = 1
	picture = "law"
	
	action_a = {
		name = "ACTION_ALLOW_MAJORITY"									#Free Market = 3
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = 2 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -6 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTION_LIMIT_MAJORITY"									#Free Market = 2
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = 1 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 2.5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -3 }

		NOT = { puppet = { country = LIT country = SOV } }
	}

		event = 2007063 #The Latvian Restoration of Independence (transitional/de facto)
		event = 2007161 #The August Coup
		exists = LAT
		NOT = { puppet = { country = LIT country = SOV } }
	}

		event = 2007161 #The August Coup

		command = { type = relation which = DFR value = -25 }

	id = 2007124
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = {	headofgovernment = 99911 } #Gorbachev
	
	date = { day = 9 month = september year = 1987 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 21 month = december year = 2012 }
	
	name = "sov_yeltsin_resignation"
	desc = "sov_yeltsin_resignation_desc"
	style = 1
	picture = "yeltsin_resign"
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007029 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = ok_yeltsin }
	}
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_SUPPORT_YELTSIN"
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007028 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = support_yeltsin }
	}
	action = { trigger = { ai = yes flag = wic }
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007029 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = ok_yeltsin }
	}
	action = { trigger = { ai = yes flag = historical }
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007029 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = ok_yeltsin }
	}
	action = { trigger = { ai = yes flag = historical }
		name = "ACTION_SUPPORT_YELTSIN"
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007028 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = support_yeltsin }
	}
	action = { trigger = { ai = yes flag = ahistorical }
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		ai_chance = 40
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007029 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = ok_yeltsin }
	}
	action = { trigger = { ai = yes flag = ahistorical }
		name = "ACTION_SUPPORT_YELTSIN"
		ai_chance = 60
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2007028 }
		#command = { type = local_setflag which = support_yeltsin }
	}
}
#########################################################################
#  The Politburo's Rebel
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 2007125
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				local_flag = ok_yeltsin
			}
			AND = {
				local_flag = yeltsin_hos
				random = 40
			}
			AND = {
				local_flag = yeltsin_fm
				random = 50
			}
			AND = {
				local_flag = yeltsin_moa
				random = 60
			}
		}
	}
	
	date = { day = 26 month = october year = 1987 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 0 month = january year = 1988 }
	
	name = "sov_yeltsin_resignation_2"
	desc = "sov_yeltsin_resignation_2_desc"
	style = 1
	picture = "boris_yeltsin1"
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_OK"
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = ok_yeltsin }
	}
}

#China receives rapprochement offer
event = {
	id = 2007205
	random = no
	country = CHC
	
	name = "rapprochement_soviets"
	desc = "rapprochement_soviets_desc"
	style = 1
	picture = "diplomatic_campaign"
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_ACCEPT"
		#trigger = { flag = tpstandard }
		ai_chance = 70
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = 150 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = ai which = "switch/chc_pro_soviet.ai" }
	}
	action = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_REFUSE"
		#trigger = { flag = tpstandard }
		ai_chance = 30
		command = { type = belligerence value = 5 }
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -150 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 2007206 }

event = {
	id = 2007215
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = {
		war = { country = SOV country = DFR }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = DDR }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = DDR }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = POL }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = POL }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = CZE }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = CZE }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = HUN }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = HUN }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = ROM }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = ROM }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						control = { province = 75 data = BUL }
						alliance = { country = SOV country = BUL }
					}
					control = { province = 75 data = SOV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1985 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 21 month = december year = 2012 }
	
	name = "West Berlin falls!"
	desc = "Our people believe even more in the final victory!"
	style = 1
	picture = "sov_restore_order"

#########################################################################
#  Restore the Warsaw Pact
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 2007226
	random = no
	country = SOV
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		OR = {
			event = 2007214 #Reinstate the Brezhnev Doctrine
			NOT = { local_flag = sinatra_doctrine } #Sinatra Doctrine
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = DDR }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = DDR }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = DDR }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = POL }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = POL }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = POL }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = CZE }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = CZE }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = CZE }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = HUN }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = HUN }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = HUN }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = ROM }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = ROM }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = ROM }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = BUL }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = BUL }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = BUL }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	decision_trigger = {
		domestic = { type = interventionism value = 7 }
	}
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			event = 2007214 #Reinstate the Brezhnev Doctrine
			NOT = { local_flag = sinatra_doctrine } #Sinatra Doctrine
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = DDR }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = DDR }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = DDR }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = POL }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = POL }
					alliance = { country = -1 country = POL }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					ideology = { type = stalinist country = CZE }
					ideology = { type = leninist country = CZE }
